--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/Gun.lua ---

--[[
    Gun (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local ContextActionService = game:GetService('ContextActionService');
local UserGameSettings = UserSettings():GetService('UserGameSettings');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local ContextActionUtility = require(script.Parent.Parent.Parent.Modules.ContextActionUtility);

local AnimationGUI;
local NetworkFunctionController;
local NetworkController;
local LookController;
local KeybindController;
local WeaponGUI;
local Trove;

local MobileCrosshair;

local DeviceUtil;

local DEFAULT_ICON = '';
local CROSSHAIR_ICON = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5764609631';
local HITMARKER_ICON = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5764742471';

local wait;
local mathRandom = math.random;
local mathMin = math.min;
local newCFrame = CFrame.new;
local anglesCFrame = CFrame.Angles;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse();

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;
local screenPointToRay = camera.ScreenPointToRay;
local UserInputService = game:GetService('UserInputService')

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local ignoreList = CollectionService:GetTagged('RayIgnore');

local GetPlayerFromCharacter;
local FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList;

local function GetMousePosDirection(startPos, range, spread: number)
    spread = math.random(-spread, spread);
    local ray;

    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        local MobileCrosshairPos = {
            X = 0;
            Y = 0;
        };

        MobileCrosshairPos.X = MobileCrosshair.AbsolutePosition.X + (MobileCrosshair.AbsoluteSize.X / 2);
        MobileCrosshairPos.Y = MobileCrosshair.AbsolutePosition.Y + (MobileCrosshair.AbsoluteSize.Y / 2);
        
        if spread then
            ray = screenPointToRay(camera, MobileCrosshairPos.X + (math.random() * (spread * 2) - spread), MobileCrosshairPos.Y + (math.random() * (spread * 2) - spread));
        else
            ray = screenPointToRay(camera, MobileCrosshairPos.X, MobileCrosshairPos.Y);
        end;
    else
        if spread then
            ray = screenPointToRay(camera, mouse.X + (math.random() * (spread * 2) - spread), mouse.Y + (math.random() * (spread * 2) - spread));
        else
            ray = screenPointToRay(camera, mouse.X, mouse.Y);
        end;
    end


    local hit, pos = FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(ray.Origin, ray.Direction * range, ignoreList);
    local direction = pos - startPos;
    local distance = direction.Magnitude + 8;
    return (direction).Unit * distance;
end;

local Gun = {};
Gun.__index = Gun;

function Gun.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Gun);

    self.AnimationCompleted = false;

    local config = require(tool.GunConfig);

    self.Character = localPlayer.Character;
    self.Head = self.Character.Head;

    self.Gun = tool;
	self.Barrel = tool.Barrel;
	self.Name = tool.Name;

    self.AutoFire = config.AutoFire;
    self.CanChangeFireMode = (self.AutoFire == true);
    self.Recoil = config.Recoil;
    self.NegativeRecoil = -self.Recoil;
    self.Debounce = config.Debounce;
    self.Range = config.Range;

    self.Ammo = tool:GetAttribute('Ammo');
	self.MaxAmmo = tool:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo');
	self.State = tool:GetAttribute('State') or "";

    self.LastShot = tick();
    self.Shooting = false;
    self.Reloading = false;

    self.ShotCount = config.ShotCount or 1 ;
    if self.ShotCount > 1 then
        self.Spread = config.Spread;
    end;

    self.MouselockConnection = nil;

    self.Trove = Trove.new();

	ignoreList[#ignoreList + 1] = self.Character;
	ignoreList[#ignoreList + 1] = self.Gun;

    return self;
end;

function Gun:RotateCamera(rotationX, rotationY, duration)
    coroutineWrap(function()
        local shotTime = self.LastShot;

        local step = mathMin(1.5 / duration, 90);
        local x = 0;

        while true do
            if self.LastShot ~= shotTime then break; end;

            x = x + step;
            x = x > 90 and 90 or x;

            local camCFrame = camera.CFrame;
            local camFocus = camera.Focus;

            local camRot = camCFrame - camCFrame.Position;
            local camDist = (camCFrame.Position - camFocus.Position).Magnitude;
            local newCamCFrame = newCFrame(camFocus.Position) * camRot * anglesCFrame(rotationX / (90 / step), rotationY / (90 / step), 0);
            camera.CFrame = newCFrame(newCamCFrame.Position, newCamCFrame.Position + newCamCFrame.LookVector) * newCFrame(0, 0, camDist);

            if x == 90 then break; end;

            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
    end)();
end;

function Gun:RecoilFunc()
    local recoil = self.Recoil;
    local rotationY = (mathRandom() - 0.5) * (recoil * 0.7);
    self:RotateCamera(recoil, rotationY, 0.08);
    wait(0.08);
    self:RotateCamera(self.NegativeRecoil, -rotationY, 0.18);
end;

function Gun:Hitmarker()
    coroutineWrap(function()
        mouse.Icon = HITMARKER_ICON;
        wait(0.2);
        mouse.Icon = CROSSHAIR_ICON;
    end)();
end;

function Gun:Shoot()
    if self.Reloading then return; end;
    if self.Ammo <= 0 then return; end;
    if self.AtEase == true then return; end;
	if (tick() - self.LastShot) < self.Debounce then return; end;
    if not self.AnimationCompleted then return; end;


	self.LastShot = tick();
	if self.Gun:FindFirstChild('ShootAnimation') then
		self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(self.Gun.ShootAnimation):Play()
	end

    local hits = {};

    for i = 1, self.ShotCount do
        local barrelPos = self.Barrel.Position;
        local headPos = self.Head.Position;

        local mouseTargetPos = mouse.Hit.p;
        local distance = (barrelPos - mouseTargetPos).Magnitude

        local spread = 0;

        if self.Spread then
            spread = self.Spread / 50 * distance
        end

        local mouseDirection = GetMousePosDirection(barrelPos, self.Range, spread);


        local hit, pos, normal = FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(barrelPos, mouseDirection, ignoreList);
        local targetHit;

        if (hit) and (not FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(headPos, barrelPos - headPos, ignoreList)) then
            table.insert(hits, {
                BarrelPos = barrelPos,
                Hit = hit,
                Pos = pos,
                Normal = normal,
                MouseDirection = mouseDirection,
                ClientHitPos = hit.Position
            });
            local hitName = hit.Name;
            if (hitName == 'Wheel') and (hit.CanCollide) then
                targetHit = hit;
                self:Hitmarker();
            elseif hitName == 'BreakableGlass' then
                targetHit = hit;
                self:Hitmarker();
            else
                local possibleChar = hit.Parent;
                if possibleChar then
                    if GetPlayerFromCharacter(possibleChar) and possibleChar.Humanoid.Health > 1 then
                        targetHit = hit;
                        self:Hitmarker();
                    end;
                end;
            end;
        end;
        --local mouseOrigin = mouse.Origin;
--[[         NetworkController.Send(
            'Gun',
            'Shoot',
            pos,
            targetHit,
            --targetHit and mouseOrigin.Position,
            --targetHit and mouseOrigin.LookVector,
            targetHit and targetHit.Position
        );
        NetworkController.Send(
            'BulletEffect',
            barrelPos,
            hit,
            pos,
            normal,
            GetMousePosDirection(barrelPos, self.Range)
        ); ]]
        task.spawn(function()
            self:RecoilFunc();
        end);
    end
    NetworkController.Send(
        'Gun',
        'Shoot',
        hits
    )
end;

function Gun:Reload()
    if self.Reloading then return; end;
    if self.Ammo == self.MaxAmmo then return; end;
    self.Reloading = true;
    
    local ammo = self.Gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
    if ammo ~= self.Ammo then
        self.Ammo = ammo;
        WeaponGUI.SetAmmo(ammo);
    end;

    NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GunReload');
    self.Reloading = false;
end;

function Gun:ChangeFireMode()
    if not self.CanChangeFireMode then return; end;
    self.AutoFire = not self.AutoFire;
    WeaponGUI.SetFireMode(self.AutoFire == true and 'Auto' or 'Semi', self.Name);
end;

function Gun:Equipped()
    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        if self.MouselockConnection then
            self.MouselockConnection:Disconnect();
            self.MouselockConnection = nil;
        end;

        MobileCrosshair.Visible = true;

        self.MouselockConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
            UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter;
            UserGameSettings.RotationType = Enum.RotationType.CameraRelative;
        end)

        self.Character.Humanoid.CameraOffset = Vector3.new(2, 0, -4);
    end
	local gun = self.Gun;

    mouse.Icon = CROSSHAIR_ICON;

    local holdAnimation = self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(gun.HoldAnimation);
	holdAnimation:Play();
	holdAnimation.KeyframeReached:connect(function(keyframeName)
		if keyframeName == "Pause" then
			holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(0)
			WeaponGUI:Enable(gun.Name, self.Ammo, gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'), 'Ammo:', self.AutoFire == true and 'Auto' or 'Semi');
            self.AnimationCompleted = true;
		end
	end)
    holdAnimation:GetMarkerReachedSignal('Pause'):Connect(function()
        holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(0)
		WeaponGUI:Enable(gun.Name, self.State or "", self.Ammo, gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'), 'Ammo:', self.AutoFire == true and 'Auto' or 'Semi');
        self.AnimationCompleted = true;
    end)

    LookController.SetMouseControl(true);

    self.Trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
        ActionName = 'Reload';
        Key = Enum.KeyCode.R;
        Description = 'Reload';
        OnPressed = function()
            self:Reload();
        end;
        CreateMobileButton = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
    }));

    if self.CanChangeFireMode then
        self.Trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
            ActionName = 'ChangeFireMode';
            Key = Enum.KeyCode.V;
            Description = 'Change Fire Mode';
            OnPressed = function()
                self:ChangeFireMode();
            end;
            CreateMobileButton = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
        })); 
    end;

    if gun:FindFirstChild('Flashlight') then
        self.Trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
            ActionName = 'GunFlashlight';
            Key = Enum.KeyCode.F;
            Description = 'Flashlight';
            OnPressed = function()
                NetworkController.Send('Gun', 'Flashlight');
            end;
            CreateMobileButton = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
        }));
    end

    if gun:FindFirstChild('AtEaseAnimation') then
        self.AtEaseAnimation = self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(gun.AtEaseAnimation);
        self.AtEaseAnimation.Looped = false;
        self.AtEaseAnimation.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action2;
        self.Trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
            ActionName = 'AtEase';
            Key = Enum.KeyCode.G;
            Description = 'At Ease';
            OnPressed = function()
                if not self.AnimationCompleted then return; end;
                if not self.AtEase then
                    self.AtEaseAnimation:Play();
                    self.AtEaseAnimation.Stopped:Once(function()
                        self.AtEase = true;
                        self.AtEaseAnimation:Play();
                        self.AtEaseAnimation:AdjustSpeed(0);
                        self.AtEaseAnimation.TimePosition = self.AtEaseAnimation.Length - 0.02;
                    end);
                else
                    self.AtEase = false;
                    self.AtEaseAnimation:AdjustSpeed(1);
                end;
            end;
            CreateMobileButton = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
        }));
    end;

    if gun:FindFirstChild('CrouchAnimation') then
        self.CrouchAnimation = self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(gun.CrouchAnimation);

        self.Trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
            ActionName = 'Crouch';
            Key = Enum.KeyCode.C;
            Description = 'Crouch';
            OnPressed = function()
                local undoCrouch = function()
                    AnimationGUI.Animated = false;
                    self.Crouching = false;
                end;
                if not self.AnimationCompleted then return; end;
                if not self.Crouching then
                    self.CrouchAnimation:Play();
                    AnimationGUI.Animated = true;
                    self.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 8;
                    self.Crouching = true;
                    self.Trove['ListenForAnimations'] = AnimationGUI.GUIAnimationStartedSignal:Connect(function()
                        if self.CrouchAnimation.IsPlaying then
                            self.CrouchAnimation:Stop();
                        end;
                    end);
                    self.Trove:Add(undoCrouch);
                else
                    AnimationGUI.Animated = false;
                    self.Trove['ListenForAnimations'] = nil;
                    self.Trove:Remove(undoCrouch);
                    self.Crouching = false;
                    self.CrouchAnimation:Stop();
                end;
                    --holdAnimation:Stop();
            end;
            CreateMobileButton = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
        }));
    end

    ContextActionUtility:BindAction('Shoot', function(actionName, userInputState)
        if userInputState ~= Enum.UserInputState.Begin then return; end;
        self:Shoot();
    end, true);

    self.Trove:Add(gun:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Ammo'):Connect(function()
        self.Ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
        WeaponGUI.SetAmmo(self.Ammo);
	end));

    self.Trove:Add(gun:GetAttributeChangedSignal('ReserveAmmo'):Connect(function()
        WeaponGUI.SetReserveAmmo(gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'));
    end));

    self.Trove:Add(function()
		ContextActionUtility:UnbindAction('Shoot');
    end);

    self.Trove:Add(function()
		holdAnimation:Stop();
		holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(1)
        if self.AtEaseAnimation then
            self.AtEaseAnimation:Stop();
            self.AtEase = false;
        end;
    end);
end;

function Gun:Activated()
    if self.AutoFire then
        self.Shooting = true;
        while self.Shooting do
			self:Shoot();
            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
    else
        self:Shoot();
    end;
end;

function Gun:Deactivated()
    self.Shooting = false;
end;

function Gun:Unequipped()
    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        if self.MouselockConnection then
            self.MouselockConnection:Disconnect();
            self.MouselockConnection = nil;
        end;
        self.Character.Humanoid.CameraOffset = Vector3.new(0,0,0);
    end
    mouse.Icon = DEFAULT_ICON;
    WeaponGUI.Disable();
    LookController.SetMouseControl(false);
    self.Shooting = false;
    self.Trove:Destroy();
    self.AnimationCompleted = false;

    local tracks = self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks();
    for _, track: AnimationTrack in tracks do
        if track.Animation:IsDescendantOf(self.Gun) then
            track:Stop();
        end;
    end;
end;

function Gun:Start()
    MobileCrosshair = WeaponGUI.MobileCrosshair;
end;

function Gun:Init()
    DeviceUtil = self.Modules.DeviceUtil;
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    LookController = self.Controllers.Character.LookController;
    AnimationGUI = self.Controllers.UI.AnimationGUI;
    KeybindController = self.Controllers.KeybindController;
    WeaponGUI = self.Controllers.UI.WeaponGUI;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    GetPlayerFromCharacter = self.Shared.GetPlayerFromCharacter;
    FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList = self.Shared.Raycast.FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList;
end;

return Gun;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/MeleeWeapon.lua ---

--[[
    MeleeWeapon (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
-- Melee Weapons
-- Khizzer
-- June 17, 2021

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkController;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local MeleeWeapon = {};
MeleeWeapon.__index = MeleeWeapon;

function MeleeWeapon.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, MeleeWeapon);
    self.Tool = tool
    self.HitAnim = localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(tool.HitAnim);
    self.Hitbox = tool.Hitbox;
    self.Cooldown = false;
    self.Hit = false;
    self.CanBreakWindows = tool:GetAttribute('CanBreakWindows') or false;

    return self;
end;

function MeleeWeapon:Equipped()
    if self.Tool:FindFirstChild('HoldAnim') then
        self.HoldAnim = localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(self.Tool.HoldAnim);
        self.HoldAnim:Play();
    end
end;

function MeleeWeapon:Activated()

    if self.Cooldown then return; end;

    self.Cooldown = true;
    if self.HoldAnim then
        self.HoldAnim:Stop();
    end;

    self.HitAnim:Play();

    self.Hit = self.Hitbox.Touched:Connect(function(part)
        local hitCharacter = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(part.Parent)
        if hitCharacter then
            NetworkController.Send('MeleeWeapon', 'CharacterHit', part.Parent.HumanoidRootPart);
            self.Hit:Disconnect();
            self.Hit = nil;
         elseif part.Name == 'BreakableGlass' and self.CanBreakWindows then
            NetworkController.Send('MeleeWeapon', 'BreakableGlassHit', part);
        end;
    end)

    self.HitAnim.Stopped:Wait();
    
    if self.HoldAnim then
        self.HoldAnim:Play();
    end;
    
    if self.Hit then
        self.Hit:Disconnect();
        self.Hit = nil
    end
    self.Cooldown = false;
end;

function MeleeWeapon:Deactivated()
end;

function MeleeWeapon:Unequipped()
    if self.HoldAnim then
        self.HoldAnim:Stop();
    end
end;

function MeleeWeapon:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController
end

return MeleeWeapon

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/PepperGun.lua ---

--[[
    PepperGun (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local ContextActionService = game:GetService('ContextActionService');

local GunService;
local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;
local LookController;
local WeaponGUI;
local Maid;

local DEFAULT_ICON = '';
local CROSSHAIR_ICON = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5764609631';
local HITMARKER_ICON = 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5764742471';

local wait;
local mathRandom = math.random;
local mathMin = math.min;
local newCFrame = CFrame.new;
local anglesCFrame = CFrame.Angles;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse();

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;
local screenPointToRay = camera.ScreenPointToRay;

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local ignoreList = CollectionService:GetTagged('RayIgnore');

local GetPlayerFromCharacter;
local FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList;

local function GetMousePosDirection(startPos, range)
    local ray = screenPointToRay(camera, mouse.X, mouse.Y);
    local hit, pos = FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(ray.Origin, ray.Direction * range, ignoreList);
    local direction = pos - startPos;
    local distance = direction.Magnitude + 8;
    return (direction).Unit * distance;
end;

local PepperGun = {};
PepperGun.__index = PepperGun;

function PepperGun.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, PepperGun);

    local config = require(tool.GunConfig);

    self.Character = localPlayer.Character;
    self.Head = self.Character.Head;

    self.Gun = tool;
    self.Barrel = tool.Barrel;

    self.AutoFire = config.AutoFire;
    self.Recoil = config.Recoil;
    self.NegativeRecoil = -self.Recoil;
    self.Debounce = config.Debounce;
    self.Range = config.Range;

    self.Ammo = tool:GetAttribute('Ammo');
    self.MaxAmmo = tool:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo');

    self.LastShot = tick();
    self.Shooting = false;
    self.Reloading = false;

    self.Maid = Maid.new();

	ignoreList[#ignoreList + 1] = self.Character;
	ignoreList[#ignoreList + 1] = self.Gun;

    return self;
end;

function PepperGun:RotateCamera(rotationX, rotationY, duration)
    coroutineWrap(function()
        local shotTime = self.LastShot;

        local step = mathMin(1.5 / duration, 90);
        local x = 0;

        while true do
            if self.LastShot ~= shotTime then break; end;

            x = x + step;
            x = x > 90 and 90 or x;

            local camCFrame = camera.CFrame;
            local camFocus = camera.Focus;

            local camRot = camCFrame - camCFrame.Position;
            local camDist = (camCFrame.Position - camFocus.Position).Magnitude;
            local newCamCFrame = newCFrame(camFocus.Position) * camRot * anglesCFrame(rotationX / (90 / step), rotationY / (90 / step), 0);
            camera.CFrame = newCFrame(newCamCFrame.Position, newCamCFrame.Position + newCamCFrame.LookVector) * newCFrame(0, 0, camDist);

            if x == 90 then break; end;

            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
    end)();
end;

function PepperGun:RecoilFunc()
    local recoil = self.Recoil;
    local rotationY = (mathRandom() - 0.5) * (recoil * 0.7);
    self:RotateCamera(recoil, rotationY, 0.08);
    wait(0.08);
    self:RotateCamera(self.NegativeRecoil, -rotationY, 0.18);
end;

function PepperGun:Hitmarker()
    coroutineWrap(function()
        mouse.Icon = HITMARKER_ICON;
        wait(0.2);
        mouse.Icon = CROSSHAIR_ICON;
    end)();
end;

function PepperGun:Shoot()
    if self.Reloading then return; end;
    if self.Ammo <= 0 then return; end;
	if (tick() - self.LastShot) < self.Debounce then return; end;

	self.LastShot = tick();
	if self.Gun:FindFirstChild('ShootAnimation') then
		self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(self.Gun.ShootAnimation):Play()
	end

    local barrelPos = self.Barrel.Position;
    local headPos = self.Head.Position;
    local hit, pos = FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(barrelPos, GetMousePosDirection(barrelPos, self.Range), ignoreList);
    local targetHit;
    if (hit) and (not FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(headPos, barrelPos - headPos, ignoreList)) then
        local possibleChar = hit.Parent;
        if possibleChar then
            if GetPlayerFromCharacter(possibleChar) and possibleChar.Humanoid.Health > 1 then
                targetHit = hit;
                self:Hitmarker();
            end;
        end;
    end;
    --local mouseOrigin = mouse.Origin;
    NetworkController.Send(
        'PepperGun',
        'Shoot',
        pos,
        targetHit,
        --[[targetHit and mouseOrigin.Position,
        targetHit and mouseOrigin.LookVector,]]
        targetHit and targetHit.Position
    );
    coroutineWrap(function()
        self:RecoilFunc();
    end)();
end;

function PepperGun:Reload()
    if self.Reloading then return; end;
    if self.Ammo == self.MaxAmmo then return; end;
    self.Reloading = true;
    NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('GunReload');
    self.Reloading = false;
end;

function PepperGun:Equipped()
    local gun = self.Gun;
    mouse.Icon = CROSSHAIR_ICON;

    local holdAnimation = self.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(gun.HoldAnimation);
	holdAnimation:Play();
	holdAnimation.KeyframeReached:connect(function(keyframeName)
		if keyframeName == "Pause" then
			holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(0)
			WeaponGUI:Enable(gun.Name, self.Ammo, gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'), 'Ammo:', 'Semi');
		end
	end)
    holdAnimation:GetMarkerReachedSignal('Pause'):Connect(function()
        holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(0)
        WeaponGUI:Enable(gun.Name, self.Ammo, gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'), 'Ammo:', 'Semi');
    end)
	
    LookController.SetMouseControl(true);

    ContextActionService:BindAction('Reload', function(actionName, userInputState)
        if userInputState ~= Enum.UserInputState.Begin then return; end;
        self:Reload();
    end, true, Enum.KeyCode.R);

    ContextActionService:BindAction('Shoot', function(actionName, userInputState)
        if userInputState ~= Enum.UserInputState.Begin then return; end;
        self:Shoot();
    end, true);

    ContextActionService:SetTitle('Shoot', 'Shoot');

    ContextActionService:SetImage('Reload', 'http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5498378510');

    self.Maid:GiveTask(gun:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Ammo'):Connect(function()
        self.Ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
        WeaponGUI.SetAmmo(self.Ammo);
    end));
    self.Maid:GiveTask(gun:GetAttributeChangedSignal('ReserveAmmo'):Connect(function()
        WeaponGUI.SetReserveAmmo(gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo'));
    end));
    self.Maid:GiveTask(function()
        ContextActionService:UnbindAction('Reload');
        ContextActionService:UnbindAction('Shoot');
    end);
    self.Maid:GiveTask(function()
		holdAnimation:Stop();
		holdAnimation:AdjustSpeed(1)
    end);
end;

function PepperGun:Activated()
    if self.AutoFire then
        self.Shooting = true;
        while self.Shooting do
			self:Shoot();
            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
    else
        self:Shoot();
    end;
end;

function PepperGun:Deactivated()
    self.Shooting = false;
end;

function PepperGun:Unequipped()
    mouse.Icon = DEFAULT_ICON;
    WeaponGUI.Disable();
    LookController.SetMouseControl(false);
    self.Shooting = false;
    self.Maid:DoCleaning();
end;

function PepperGun:Start()

end;

function PepperGun:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    LookController = self.Controllers.Character.LookController;
    WeaponGUI = self.Controllers.UI.WeaponGUI;
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    GetPlayerFromCharacter = self.Shared.GetPlayerFromCharacter;
    FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList = self.Shared.Raycast.FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList;
end;

return PepperGun;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/PepperSpray.lua ---

--[[
    PepperSpray (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local Send;

local PepperSpray = {};
PepperSpray.__index = PepperSpray;

function PepperSpray.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, PepperSpray);

    self.Hitbox = tool.Hitbox;
    self.Hit = nil;
    self.Spraying = false;

    return self;
end;

function PepperSpray:Disable()
    if self.Spraying then
        self.Spraying = false;
        self.Hit:Disconnect();
        self.Hit = nil;
        Send('PepperSpray', 'Disable');
    end;
end;

function PepperSpray:Equipped()

end;

function PepperSpray:Activated()
    Send('PepperSpray', 'Enable');
    self.Hit = self.Hitbox.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        local hitPlayer = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(hit.Parent);
        if hitPlayer then
            Send('PepperSpray', 'Spray', hit);
        end;
    end);
    self.Spraying = true;
end;

function PepperSpray:Deactivated()
    self:Disable();
end;

function PepperSpray:Unequipped()
    self:Disable();
end;

function PepperSpray:Init()
    Send = self.Controllers.NetworkController.Send;
end;

return PepperSpray;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/Placeable.lua ---

--[[
    Placeable (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');

local NetworkController;
local Maid;

local PLACE_EVENT;
local PLACE_OFFSET = CFrame.new(0, 0, -3.5);
local RAY_DIRECTION = Vector3.new(0, -5, 0);

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local placeables = ReplicatedStorage.Placeables;

local postSimulation = RunService.Heartbeat;

local function SetModelTransparency(model, transparency)
    local primaryPart = model.PrimaryPart;
    for i, v in next, model:GetDescendants() do
        if (v:IsA('BasePart')) and (v ~= primaryPart) then
            v.Transparency = transparency;
        end;
    end;
    model:SetAttribute('Transparency', transparency);
end;

local Raycast;

local Placeable = {};
Placeable.__index = Placeable;

function Placeable.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Placeable);

    local char = localPlayer.Character;
    self.RootPart = char.HumanoidRootPart;

    self.Model = placeables[tool:GetAttribute('Model')];
    self.ModelHalfSize = Vector3.new(0, self.Model.PrimaryPart.Size.Y * 0.5, 0);
    self.MarkerModel = nil;
    self.IgnoreList = {};

    self.Maid = Maid.new();

    return self;
end;

function Placeable:Equipped()
    self.MarkerModel = self.Model:Clone();
    SetModelTransparency(self.MarkerModel, 0.5);
    for i, v in next, self.MarkerModel:GetDescendants() do
        if (v:IsA('BasePart')) then
            v.CanCollide = false;
        end;
    end;
    self.MarkerModel.Parent = workspace;

    self.IgnoreList = {self.MarkerModel};

    self.Maid:GiveTask(postSimulation:Connect(function()
        local rootPart = self.RootPart;
        local raycastResult = Raycast((rootPart.CFrame * PLACE_OFFSET).Position, RAY_DIRECTION, self.IgnoreList);
        if raycastResult then
            if self.MarkerModel:GetAttribute('Transparency') ~= 0.5 then
                SetModelTransparency(self.MarkerModel, 0.5);
            end;
            self.MarkerModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(
                CFrame.new(raycastResult.Position + self.ModelHalfSize) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(rootPart.Orientation.Y), 0)
            );
        else
            if self.MarkerModel:GetAttribute('Transparency') ~= 1 then
                SetModelTransparency(self.MarkerModel, 1);
            end;
        end;
    end));
end;

function Placeable:Activated()
    if not self.MarkerModel then return; end;
    if self.MarkerModel:GetAttribute('Transparency') == 1 then return; end;

    NetworkController.Send(PLACE_EVENT, self.MarkerModel.PrimaryPart.CFrame);
end;

function Placeable:Deactivated()

end;

function Placeable:Unequipped()
    self.Maid:DoCleaning();
    if self.MarkerModel then
        self.MarkerModel:Destroy();
        self.MarkerModel = nil;
    end;
    self.IgnoreList = {};
end;

function Placeable:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast.Cast;
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Placeable;
    PLACE_EVENT = constants.PLACE_EVENT;
end;

return Placeable;

    PlaceableIdentifier (ModuleScript)

    return self
end;

end;

function PlaceableIdentifier:Unequipped()

end;

function PlaceableIdentifier:Activated()
    local target = MouseTarget.Get(50, {localPlayer.Character})
    local model = target and target.Parent;

    if not model then return; end;
    if not model:GetAttribute('PlacedBy') then return; end;

    Notification.new('Placeable identifier', model:GetAttribute('PlacedBy'));
end;

    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Modules/Tools/RadarGun.lua ---

--[[
    RadarGun (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Modules → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:57
]]
local MouseTarget;
local Maid;

local GUI_INSET_Y = game:GetService('GuiService'):GetGuiInset().Y;
local RAY_LENGTH = 800;

local mathFloor = math.floor;
local fromOffset = UDim2.fromOffset;
local findFirstAncestor = workspace.FindFirstAncestor;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse();

local radarGunGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('RadarGunGUI');
local UIScale = radarGunGUI.UIScale;
local mainFrame = radarGunGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;
local speedLabel = bodyFrame.SpeedLabel;
local topSpeedLabel = bodyFrame.TopSpeedLabel;

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local ConvertSpeed;

local RadarGun = {};
RadarGun.__index = RadarGun;

function RadarGun.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, RadarGun);

    self.HoldAnim = localPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(tool.HoldAnimation);
    self.TopSpeed = 0;
    self.SpeedLabel = tool.Speed.SpeedGUI.SpeedLabel;
	self.TopSpeedLabel = tool.TopSpeed.TopSpeedGUI.TopSpeedLabel;

	self.Maid = Maid.new();

    return self;
end;

function RadarGun:Equipped()
    local toolSpeedLabel = self.SpeedLabel;
	local toolTopSpeedLabel = self.TopSpeedLabel;

    self.HoldAnim:Play();
	radarGunGUI.Enabled = true;

	self.Maid:GiveTask(postSimulation:Connect(function()
		mainFrame.Position = fromOffset((mouse.X / UIScale.Scale) + 17, (mouse.Y / UIScale.Scale) + GUI_INSET_Y);
		local mouseTarget = MouseTarget.Get(RAY_LENGTH, {localPlayer.Character});
		if mouseTarget then
			local isCar = findFirstAncestor(mouseTarget, 'Body') or findFirstAncestor(mouseTarget, 'Chassis');
			if isCar then
				local speed = mathFloor(ConvertSpeed(mouseTarget.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude));
				speedLabel.Text = speed .. ' KPH';
				toolSpeedLabel.Text = speed;
				if speed > self.TopSpeed then
					self.TopSpeed = speed;
					topSpeedLabel.Text = speed .. ' KPH';
					toolTopSpeedLabel.Text = speed;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end));
end;

function RadarGun:Activated()

end;

function RadarGun:Deactivated()

end;

function RadarGun:Unequipped()
	self.HoldAnim:Stop();
	radarGunGUI.Enabled = false;
	self.Maid:DoCleaning();
	self.TopSpeed = 0;
	speedLabel.Text = '0 KPH';
	topSpeedLabel.Text = '0 KPH';
	self.SpeedLabel.Text = '0';
	self.TopSpeedLabel.Text = '0';
end;

function RadarGun:Start()

end;

function RadarGun:Init()
	MouseTarget = self.Modules.MouseTarget;
	Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
    ConvertSpeed = self.Shared.ConvertSpeed;
end;

return RadarGun;

-- Repair Tool
-- Khizzer
-- September 10, 2021

local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local RepairTool = {}
RepairTool.__index = RepairTool;

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local NetworkController;
local MouseTarget;

function RepairTool.new(tool)
    local self = setmetatable({}, RepairTool);

    local char = localPlayer.Character;
    self.RootPart = char.HumanoidRootPart;

    return self;
end;

function RepairTool:Equipped()
end;

function RepairTool:Unequipped()
end;

function RepairTool:Activated()
    local mouseTarget, pos = MouseTarget.Get(25, {localPlayer.Character});
    if mouseTarget and (mouseTarget:FindFirstAncestor('Body')) and ((self.RootPart.Position - pos).Magnitude <= 10) then
        local body = mouseTarget:FindFirstAncestor('Body');
        local car = body.Parent;
        NetworkController.Send('RepairCar', car);
    end;

end;

function RepairTool:Deactivated()
end;

function RepairTool:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    MouseTarget = self.Modules.MouseTarget;
end;


return RepairTool
